Paris Morning Post's Editorial Criticism of the International Arbitration Treaty

Only Eight Countries Have Formally Joined in Two Years

Important Disputes Are All Excluded from the Scope of Arbitration

World Society Translation Paris Morning Post Editor-in-Chief Lao Changnai recently wrote an article saying that arbitration, security, and disarmament are the three cornerstones of the future temple of peace. Regarding this level, everyone in Geneva agrees, but everyone has different opinions on the order in which these three cornerstones should be laid. Finally, Lord Cecil proposed that these three stones be placed in the soil at the same time.

I do not want to be influenced by this controversy, but I want to point out the current position of one of the three cornerstones, that is, the stone of arbitration, which is the main cornerstone of the temple of peace and the one that causes the least difficulty in the controversy. An expert in Geneva recently told me that (for a doctrine as fair and simple as international arbitration, the result of two years of discussion by thirty or forty countries is only this, which is really disappointing. This is like a ball losing its roundness due to excessive transportation.)

International arbitration is undoubtedly one of the fairest and simplest doctrines in the world. There is no doubt that where there are humans, there are disputes, so there must be an arbitration court to resolve all disputes between humans. On this point, all participants in international conferences agree. However, when it comes to writing this agreement in black ink on white paper, a kind of evil wind blows around the drafters, so that the drafters' pens are incompatible with words, and the words are incompatible with meaning. Everyone sees this as a huge object, and everyone wants to participate in its creation, so the contention arises again.

The so-called (General Treaty for the Resolution of International Disputes by Arbitration) has encountered the above situation in Geneva. After some intermittent discussions on the treaty, Sweden suddenly proposed that judicial disputes and political disputes should be distinguished. Disputes are disputes, so why should some disputes be excluded from the scope of disputes? It is incomprehensible to ordinary people. Do some disputes not contain the same crisis that can lead to war?

Therefore, Sweden proposed that judicial disputes be referred to the International Court of Justice in The Hague, and political disputes be referred to a special conciliation committee, and the administrative council of the League of Nations has the final power of judgment. Among the countries, such as Britain, enthusiastically supported the division of judicial disputes and political disputes into two categories, and other countries suggested two classifications and then set exceptions. After two years of revision and revision, this (General Treaty for the Resolution of International Disputes by Arbitration) was officially released in June 1928. The treaty has 47 articles divided into four chapters. Its content is a mixture of regulations and procedures. However, in this mixture, one thing is extremely clear, that is, Article 39 stipulates that all countries can avoid arbitration by the following excuses: A. Disputes arising before joining the General Treaty are not arbitrated. B. Disputes concerning matters of exclusive national judgment allowed by international public law are not arbitrated. C. Disputes concerning special events such as territorial law are not arbitrated. Alas, at this point, the general public will again call out to the sky and ask, since the above three items of disputes have been excluded from the scope of arbitration, what disputes are left out for arbitration?

However, this is not the worst. The worst thing is that this kind of troublesome discussion and careful drafting of the (General Treaty for the Resolution of International Disputes by Arbitration) is actually ignored by the people and governments of the world. Readers, you also know those forty countries that call themselves members of the League of Nations and publish peace theories every year. How many countries have formally notified the League of Nations Secretariat that they have complied with the General Arbitration Treaty? In fact, there are only eight countries, namely Sweden, Belgium, Denmark, Norway, the Netherlands, Finland, Luxembourg, and Spain. France is about to join without a doubt because the French lower house has unanimously resolved to order the government to join the treaty, and the upper house will only approve it sooner or later. As such, after two years of strong time, only nine countries have recognized arbitration to resolve disputes, while Britain and its colonies, as well as Germany, Italy, and Hungary, and the countries that are loudly advocating immediate disarmament, have not yet joined the ranks of approval.

At this point, we can assert that international arbitration has made very slow progress in the past two years. Assuming that this is one of the cornerstones of the temple of peace, it is an extremely unstable cornerstone that can only be used to build a paper house on it.

Question of Establishing Customs in Hong Kong

Opinions of the Guangdong Customs Superintendent

Smuggling of goods along the coast of Hong Kong is becoming increasingly rampant, resulting in a significant loss of national tax revenue. In order to prevent tax evasion, the Ministry of Finance instructed the Inspector General of Customs to go to Hong Kong to negotiate the establishment of a customs office there to prevent smuggling. A draft agreement has been negotiated and completed. It is reported that Weng Guiqing, the Guangdong Customs Superintendent, sent a telegram to the ministry yesterday, expressing strong support for this agreement and emphasizing that smuggling in the south is increasing daily, and establishing a customs office as soon as possible is necessary to prevent it. The telegram is recorded as follows: (It has been examined that the draft agreement for the establishment of a customs office in Hong Kong was submitted to the Ministry for review, and all clauses seem fair and reasonable. The Hong Kong side benefits greatly from the principle in Clause 16, which aims to provide convenience to merchants and promote the commercial and economic development of the port. However, in Item A of that clause, Chinese goods imported from Chinese treaty ports into Hong Kong or re-exported to China from the same or other treaty ports are exempt from import duties, provided they are in their original packaging and have not been altered. However, they may also apply to the Chinese customs for permission to repack. If the repackaging process is not closely monitored by personnel, there is a risk of abuse. In Item B, the period for which import duties paid on foreign goods imported into China can be refunded when re-exported from Hong Kong within three years seems too long. I have discussed this with you in person before, and recently the Inspector General of Customs came to the provincial capital to meet with me. I also suggested that these two points should be considered further. I was then informed that an agreement had been reached with the Hong Kong government to allow the establishment of customs warehouses in Hong Kong, managed by the Chinese customs. Goods stored in the warehouses would be sealed by the customs for all entry and exit, and repackaging could be inspected at any time, eliminating any concerns. If this is implemented, it will be more complete. According to current investigations, nearly one-third of smuggled goods are in southern China. After the new tax is implemented, smuggling will inevitably increase. It seems that this agreement should be approved and a customs office established as soon as possible to remedy the situation. If it is not yet perfect, a trial period of one year can be set, after which the agreement can be revised to allow for adjustments. I hope you will consider and implement this. Furthermore, I would like to state that the customs office is responsible for managing the inspection of goods entering and exiting several provinces in South China, and this is a very important responsibility. Especially in the initial stages, it is necessary to appoint special, honest, and competent Chinese and foreign personnel to handle the work in order to achieve effective results and prevent corruption. I hope that you will be able to see through this. After the establishment of a customs office in Hong Kong, Chinese and foreign smugglers will inevitably change their methods and use a large number of smaller ships to transport goods and smuggle them into the mainland through other ports, such as Guangzhou Bay, Taiwan, and Macau. It is necessary to continue to carry out inspections or establish customs offices in these ports, or dispatch patrol boats to investigate and crack down on smuggling, in order to achieve comprehensive control. Otherwise, if we only focus on one area and neglect others, we will still not be able to achieve the desired results. This is my humble opinion, and I hope you will consider it. Submitted by your subordinate, Weng Guiqing.)

Rampant Activities of Korean Communists in Yanbian

Tragic Case of Burning Down Yanji County School and Burning an Entire Family to Death

Jilin Correspondence: There are tens of thousands of Koreans living in Yanbian. Among them, some of the lower-class elements have become increasingly depraved, leading to the rampant activities of Korean communists in the area. Despite repeated earnest warnings from the Jilin Provincial Government, there has been little improvement. On the 18th of last month, the 29th County-Run School in Liushuhezi, Chongli Township, Yanji County, was burned down by communist bandits, resulting in the tragic death of many people. Upon receiving the report, the County Education Bureau immediately forwarded it to the County Government, ordering the police to block and suppress the bandits. At the same time, they telegraphed Zhao Yuling, the principal of the Ninth School, to investigate and report the details. According to the reply, it was confirmed that at 12:00 PM on November 18, more than 20 communist bandits suddenly arrived at Liushuhezi and surrounded the 29th County-Run School. They poured cotton and straw with coal oil and set fires on all four sides. In an instant, the fire spread rapidly, and all nine school buildings were reduced to ashes. A total of five people were burned to death, including the principal, Li Houye, his wife, Wang, a one-year-old child, and a three-year-old child. In addition, Li Hougui, the principal's uncle, who was visiting the school, was also burned to death. A school employee named Hou Yuankai managed to escape from the fire. He went to the home of a farmer named Li in the nearby village and asked for a cotton quilt to cover his body before leaving the village. His whereabouts are unknown. Teacher Zheng Bingshi and his younger brother, Zheng Bingzhi, managed to escape with only their hair burned. His wife crawled out of the fire, but her head was struck with a hole in her left forehead by bandits, causing severe bleeding. Her condition is critical. Currently, there are five corpses in the school, with charred heads, broken legs, and broken arms, covered with hemp cloth and guarded by the village chief, Xuan Jiyi. Zheng's wife was carried to a neighbor's house.

To provide medical treatment. He was staying in the western room of the main house, while the principal and his family were staying in the eastern room. The school employee and Li Hougui were staying in the middle room. As for how the school employee Hou Yuankai and his wife and brother escaped, he did not know. He had no weapons and dared not go to the rescue. He fled to the back mountain to take refuge. When he went out, he saw four or five bandits with white upper bodies and blue lower bodies. He could see them clearly because of the firelight. He only returned at 10:00 PM this afternoon. He could not provide further details. An investigation found that the principal's body was found crawling out of the front window of the eastern room of the main house. His left leg and both arms were broken, and his head was half-burned. It was speculated that he must have tried to jump out of the window but was struck with broken arms by the bandits. Then, the fire burned fiercely, and he died lying on the window. The wind was strong outside the window, and the fire was blown inward by the wind, so his hair was not completely burned. His left leg was broken, perhaps because it was crushed by falling beams. After the bandits left, several leaflets were posted on the school wall, pasted with potato paste. (A) About in early May, because it was not appropriate to stay at a friend's house for too long, so I moved out. (Q) Did you see Ye often at the hotel? (A) Yes, often. (Q) Why did you move to the Barras Hotel and when did you move there? (A) Because the rooms at the Barras Hotel were larger and the indoor air was better. There was also a bathroom, so I could take a bath every day and feel more comfortable. I moved there around the beginning of August. (Q) Did you go with Ye when you remitted 7,050 yuan in cash from the Bank of Communications? (A) Lengyun went alone. I used to handle deposits and withdrawals at the Bank of Communications here myself, but sometimes I asked him to do it for me. (Q) Do you remember the date? (A) About two days before I left. (Q) Who kept the seal and the remittance slip before you left? (A) He took the seal away on the day of the withdrawal and never returned it. As for the remittance slip, he also said that it would be safer for him to keep it. I did not object, so he took it with him. (Q) Did Ye accompany you to Beiping or just send you to Changchun? (A) We went to Beiping together. (Q) Did you have any arguments in the car before arriving at Shuangcheng? (A) No. (Q) What else happened before arriving at Shuangcheng Station? (A) At that time, we were sitting in the second-class carriage. He asked me for the key to open my suitcase to take out his pants to change. In fact, he did not have any pants in my suitcase. Now I understand that he was just using this as an excuse to trick me out of my key. I probably had eight or nine keys. The keys to my suitcase at my home in Beiping were also inside. (Q) What was Ye's attitude like before arriving at Shuangcheng Station? (A) He looked flustered and very unnatural. I even joked and said, "Lengyun, what's wrong? Why are you so flustered and look so bad? Are you going to die?" (Q) Besides the 7,050 yuan remittance slip, did Ye know that you had other money? (A) Now I understand that I was unintentional, but he was intentional. He had already asked me how much money I had (about 20,000 yuan deposited somewhere), and he was very attentive to the date when the interest was due. (Q) How did he trick you into getting off the train when you arrived at Shuang Station? (A) He said that there was a very nice place in Shuangcheng that I had to see. The express train only stops for ten minutes, but this is a slow train and will stop for sixty minutes. I didn't want to get off the train, but he forced me to get off. So I put on my coat and got off with him. Because the road was slippery, he held my arm to help me walk. We walked west and then turned north. Suddenly, he tripped me and shot me in the back. I knew I was attacked. Although I felt very painful, I didn't dare to groan for fear that he would fire two more shots. After shooting, he turned around to look at me, but he believed that I was dead. (Q) How were you rescued? (A) After a short while, someone was walking with a lantern. I shouted for help. The person wanted to report to the police at the station first and then come back to carry me. I was afraid that Ye would harm me again, so I asked him to help me. I also reluctantly endured the pain and walked. (Q) Why did you get off the train with Ye and walk west of the railway? Weren't you afraid that Ye had ulterior motives? (A) It's easy to know a person's face but not their heart. I never thought that he was a prosecutor who knew the law but broke it and dared to plot for money and kill people. He is truly a disgrace to the judiciary. (Q) What is your attitude towards Ye now? (A) I treated him well. Now, as far as I am concerned, I am already dead. My survival is my good fortune. I heard that the court is still investigating and has not yet made a judgment. If the court is lenient, I will hire a lawyer to appeal to the high court after I am discharged from the hospital. (Q) It is rumored that you have a lover in Beiping. Is that true? What is his name? (A) It is true that I have another friend named Liu Dingshu, but I will not tell you his name. (Q) Does Ye know about him? (A) Yes, he knows.

As for Ye Yixiong, he was sent to the Binjiang District Court on the 26th. The court has held two hearings in the past week. Ye's testimony is the same as before. He still does not admit to the murder. The court sent prosecutors to the Central Hospital twice to record Zhang Liqing's testimony. Due to medical restrictions, the actual testimony has not yet been recorded. The Northeast Supreme Court has sent personnel to Harbin to investigate the truth. It is possible that he will be transferred to the Shenyang District Court for trial to avoid collusion at the same level. Ye is still being held in the detention center after entering the Daowai Court (1st).

Full Text of the Family Law in the Civil Code (Continued)

Passed by the Legislative Yuan in the Third Reading

(Article 989: If a marriage violates the provisions of Article 980, the parties or their legal representatives may petition the court for annulment, but if the parties have reached the age specified in that article or are pregnant, they may not petition for annulment. (Article 990) If a marriage violates the provisions of Article 984, the legal representative may petition the court for annulment, but if more than six months have passed since they became aware of the facts, or more than one year has passed since the marriage, or if they are pregnant, they may not petition for annulment. (Article 991) If a marriage violates the provisions of Article 984, the ward or their close relatives may petition the court for annulment, but if more than one year has passed since the marriage, they may not petition for annulment. (Article 992) If a marriage violates the provisions of Article 985, interested parties may petition the court for annulment, but they may not petition for annulment after the previous marriage relationship has been terminated. (Article 993) If a marriage violates the provisions of Article 986, the former spouse may petition the court for annulment, but if more than one year has passed since the marriage, they may not petition for annulment. (Article 994) If a marriage violates the provisions of Article 987, the former husband or his lineal relatives may petition the court for annulment, but if more than six months have passed since the termination of the previous marriage relationship, or if they are pregnant after remarriage, they may not petition for annulment. (Article 995) If one of the parties to a marriage is impotent at the time of the marriage and cannot be cured, the other party may petition the court for annulment, but if more than one year has passed since they became aware that they cannot be cured, they may not petition for annulment. (Article 996) If one of the parties to a marriage was unconscious or mentally disordered at the time of the marriage, they may petition the court for annulment within six months after the restoration of normalcy. (Article 997) A person who marries as a result of fraud or coercion may petition the court for annulment within six months after the discovery of the fraud or the cessation of coercion. (Article 998) The effect of the annulment of a marriage does not have retroactive effect. (Article 999) If one of the parties suffers damages as a result of the invalidity or annulment of a marriage, they may claim compensation from the other party, but this does not apply if the other party is not at fault. In the circumstances mentioned in the preceding paragraph, even if there is no property damage, the injured party may claim compensation for a reasonable amount, but only if the injured party is not at fault. The right to claim under the preceding paragraph may not be assigned or inherited, but this does not apply if it has been promised by contract or litigation has been initiated. Section 3 Common Effects of Marriage (Article 1000) The wife takes the husband's surname with her own surname, and the husband who marries into the wife's family takes the wife's surname with his own surname, but this does not apply if the parties have otherwise agreed. (Article 1001) Husband and wife have a mutual obligation to live together, but this does not apply if there is a legitimate reason for not being able to live together. (Article 1002) The wife takes the husband's domicile as her domicile, and the husband who marries into the wife's family takes the wife's domicile as his domicile. (Article 1003) Husband and wife are mutual agents for daily household affairs. If one of the husband and wife abuses the agency in the preceding paragraph, the other party may limit it, but may not oppose bona fide third parties. Section 4 Marital Property System Subsection 1 General Provisions (Article 1004) Husband and wife may, before or after marriage, choose one of the statutory property systems prescribed in this law as their marital property system by contract. (Article 1005) If husband and wife have not entered into a marital property system contract, the statutory property system shall be their marital property system unless otherwise provided in this law. (Article 1006) If the parties to the conclusion, alteration, or revocation of a marital property system contract are minors or persons under interdiction, they shall obtain the consent of their legal representatives. (Article 1007) The conclusion, alteration, or revocation of a marital property system contract shall be in writing. (Article 1008) The conclusion, alteration, or revocation of a marital property system contract may not be used to oppose third parties unless it is registered. The registration mentioned in the preceding paragraph shall be determined by law separately. (Article 1009) When one of the husband and wife is declared bankrupt, their marital property system shall naturally become a separate property system. (Article 1010) In any of the following circumstances, the court shall, at the request of one of the husband and wife, declare a change to a separate property system: (1) When one of the husband and wife is legally obligated to pay for household expenses but fails to do so. (2) When the property of one of the husband or wife is insufficient to pay off their debts, or the total property of the husband and wife is insufficient to pay off debts. (3) When one of the husband and wife is legally required to obtain the consent of the other party for the disposal of property, but the other party refuses to consent without a legitimate reason. (Article 1011) When a creditor has attached the property of one of the husband and wife but has not been paid, the court may, at the request of the creditor, declare a change to a separate property system. (Article 1012) Husband and wife may, during the continuation of the marriage relationship, abolish their property contract or change to another agreed property system by contract. (To be continued)

Local Correspondence

Fengxian

The Salt Transport Deputy’s Suppression of Salty and Adulterated Salt: The coastal residents of this county mostly rely on salt production for a living. Each household owns salt pans and purchases salt from factories by the catty for their livelihood. However, the weighers at the salt factories routinely demand petty fees from the salt producers when they deliver salt to the factory. Otherwise, they suppress the weight, reporting less than the actual amount, even deducting half. The difference can be several times the amount. Even if customary fees are paid, they still suppress two or three catties as "scale residue." If the shortage is not made up, not only is it deducted from the salt price and compensation pursued, but they also falsely accuse the salt producers of private sales, arresting and fining them. The salt producers’ grievances are hard to express, and they all complain bitterly. Therefore, representatives were once sent to petition the county party headquarters, calling for action. Consequently, the headquarters, in conjunction with the party headquarters of coastal counties, requested the province to forward a report to the salt authorities, urging strict suppression, which was recorded. It is now known that the Songjiang Salt Transport Deputy Envoy and the Audit Office have received a clear order to investigate and prohibit these practices, and four improvement measures have been formulated for salt deliveries to factories and distributed for compliance. Furthermore, the Transport Office has also ordered Qing Yuan and other salt yards to strictly suppress the long-standing malpractice of adulteration during salt delivery by salt producers. If such situations are discovered, the factories are authorized to detain and confiscate the salt.

Songjiang

Kidnappers Escorting Kidnapped Victims to Songjiang, Fengjing: Kidnapper Yao Jinshan specializes in kidnapping for ransom in areas near Fengjing, including Shangnanbang, Jiaodiaowan, and Jiezixu. The cases are numerous. Inspector Yang Shijie of the Public Security Bureau recently obtained information from informant Cai A'hai and captured Yao Jinshan in Shanghai. He returned to Songjiang to report to the county government and, with an official document, escorted Yao Jinshan back from Shanghai yesterday. According to his confession, he committed four kidnapping cases involving Yin Qingyun and others and hid two guns in Linjia Bang, Fengjing. He was escorted there to retrieve the weapons, which were then returned to Songjiang. Two Fengjing residents, Chen Liangen and Lu Yuyun, who went to Yao to negotiate ransom notes, allegedly for a case where they had agreed on a ransom price of six hundred yuan to be paid in three installments, were also apprehended for interrogation.

Suzhou

High Court Changes Prison Wardens: The High Court announced yesterday (the 6th) that Wang Kaiji, prison warden of Jiangpu County, has been approved to resign and has been relieved of his post. Xiang Jiahuan, prison warden of Guanyun County, is ordered to take over the vacant post. The vacant post of prison warden of Guanyun County will be filled by Sun Jifan.

Refugees from Suxian Passing Through: Yesterday (the 6th), over one hundred refugees from Suxian, Anhui, arrived in Suzhou's Fengqiao on foot from Xushuguan. They are scheduled to leave the border today (the 7th). Upon learning of this, the Public Security Bureau dispatched a team to maintain order.

Robbery at Zhangjiaqiao, Hengjing: The home of Qian Songqing, a resident of Zhangjiaqiao, Hengjing, was suddenly attacked by seven or eight robbers armed with wooden sticks and iron rulers the night before last. They ransacked the house for about an hour before fleeing. Yesterday, the Eighth Sub-bureau in charge reported the case to the bureau for investigation.

Collection of Rush Tax Officially Commences: The quota for rush tax in Wuxian has been approved for actual collection at 95%. The Finance Bureau has set up collection counters on the 11th of this month to commence collection. Each lower tax silver tael will be converted to collect the regular provincial and county taxes, together with the four- and five-cent surcharges, for a total of 2 yuan, 1 jiao, 4 fen, 2 li, and 2.5 hao in silver dollars. In addition, an order has been received to collect the Songjiang dredging fee of 2 jiao in silver and the county public security fee of 3 jiao, 5 fen in silver dollars, plus a land tax for road construction of 5 fen per mu. This amounts to a total surcharge of 5 jiao or more in silver dollars per upper and lower tax. Therefore, each lower tax tael will be converted to 3 yuan, 1 jiao, 9 fen, 2 li, and 2.5 hao in silver dollars. Each picul of tax rice will be converted to collect the regular provincial and county taxes, together with the four-cent and five-hao surcharges, for a total of 5 yuan, 2 jiao, 2 fen, and 5 li in silver dollars. Furthermore, an order has been received to add 2 yuan in silver for the rice conversion tax, plus a surcharge of 1 yuan in silver for local subsidies, 7 jiao in silver dollars for the county public security fee, 5 jiao in silver dollars for the defense corps fee, 1 yuan and 3 jiao in silver dollars for the education land tax, 2 jiao and 4 fen in silver dollars for the agricultural improvement land tax, and 1 yuan and 1 jiao and 5 fen in silver for the local subsidy land tax. This amounts to a total conversion of 12 yuan, 1 jiao, 1 fen, and 5 li in silver dollars per picul of tax rice. The bureau has also set up sub-counters in the East and West Mountains, limiting the payment period to two months from the start of collection. Late payments will be subject to late fees.

Wuxi

Latest News on the Liyang Land Tax Embezzlement Case: Regarding the Liyang County Magistrate Zheng Chengyuan and Finance Bureau Chief Pan Bin's land tax embezzlement case, the individuals involved have been arrested and detained by the provincial government and transferred to the local court. After four interrogations by the prosecutor's office, Prosecutor Yan, accompanied by clerk Wang Xia Hun and bailiffs, secretly went to Liyang to investigate the truth of the case from all relevant parties. They returned to the province the day before yesterday and have obtained concrete leads. A full investigation of witnesses will be conducted on the 6th. Regarding previous reports that Zheng Chengyuan allegedly harbored grudges against Wang Pingling and others who reported the case, an investigation of the accounts of the Liyang Park Construction Committee has been approved by the Civil Affairs Department, stating roughly: "(The report from former Liyang County Magistrate Zheng Chengyuan regarding the investigation of the accounts of the Liyang Park Construction Committee has been outstanding for a long time. Please send personnel to secretly investigate and strictly apprehend any reactionary elements.) The content of the report is noted. Order the new county magistrate of Liyang to continue to investigate and handle the matter in detail." Therefore, the outcome of the case will depend on the findings of the new county magistrate, Yuan Guanying. It is also heard that the construction accounts of Liyang Park have been publicly audited and individually reviewed by various local agencies and local figures for half a year. After more than two hundred sessions, it was finally decided that representatives from five agencies would sign and seal a receipt for Wang Pingling to hold. The content of which, cannot be speculated by outsiders.

Labor Strike in Wuxi Silk Factories Gradually Calming Down: After the labor strike broke out in silk factories throughout the county, it has been four days, causing significant losses to the factory owners and much suffering to the laborers. A small number of troublemakers are truly guilty of unforgivable crimes. Various agencies, including the Party, government, and labor unions, have made every effort to mediate, and the situation has shown signs of easing. It is hoped that this will bring about a peaceful resolution. Yesterday (the 6th), silk factories in the Zhoushanbang area, such as Qianfeng, Ruichang, Yuanfeng, Yuanyi, and those near the Gongyun Bridge, such as Gansheng and Gantai, as well as Jinji in Ximen, all sounded the siren and resumed work as usual. All the female workers entered the factories to work. Outside Nanmen, except for Minfeng Model Silk Factory, which has never been drawn into the vortex and has continued to operate as usual, other factories, such as Yulun, also resumed work yesterday morning and were operating safely. However, factories such as Yongtai and Zhenyi have not yet resumed work. It is expected that factories outside Dongmen, such as Yufeng, will also resume work across the board today. In addition, the Provincial Party Headquarters dispatched Commissioner Sun Dan Chen to Wuxi to investigate and handle the labor strike as circumstances permit. After arriving in Wuxi, Commissioner Sun immediately discussed everything with the various members of the County Party Headquarters, as well as County Magistrate Pan and the members of the Labor Consolidation Association, regarding the strict punishment and thorough investigation of the few labor thugs who incited the strike in order to maintain the labor movement.

Fourteenth Sub-bureau Chief Accused: Xun Dexing, chief of the Fourteenth Sub-bureau of Public Security in Zhangshe Town, Seventeenth District (Fuan Township), led police officers to arrest eight opium smokers, including Yao Jiqin and Zhenxi, in the Yuxiu opium den in Hutai Village of the township the day before yesterday. They also seized a large amount of opium and red pills and brought them to the bureau. It is unknown how, but later, through the mediation of Sheng Agou, an investigating police officer of the bureau, each opium offender paid 50 yuan to settle the matter. This was discovered by local residents Wang Zixian and Li Zhongying, who believed that Xun Dexing, the chief of the sub-bureau, had illegally released the opium offenders by bribery. Yesterday, they jointly filed a complaint with the county government, requesting that personnel be sent to investigate and strictly punish according to law.

Negotiations for Swindled Huge Sum: Zha Hongyu, a resident of Song Xuxiang, Fangquan Town, Fourteenth District (Kaihua Township), recently had a fanciful idea and, under the name of the Far East Foreign Firm, swindled more than 1,000 silver dollars and more than ten mu of farmland from several nearby villagers, including Guo Fengming and Xu Xiangzhou. The day before yesterday, Guo and others discovered the flaw and realized they had been cheated. They immediately rushed to Xu Hongyu's home for serious negotiations. However, Xu had already heard the news and fled secretly. Guo and others had no choice but to twist Hongyu's sister, Xu Fuxian, into the responsible public security sub-bureau and deliver her to the county public security bureau for interrogation.

Verdict on the Thirty-Six Load of Opium Case: The Third Detachment of the Sixth Team of the Second District of the Water Police stationed in Wuxi previously seized thirty-six loads of opium on a boat in the Goose Town Pond area and arrested the main offenders Yao Atu and Yao Shunfu. They were tried in the county. Yesterday, Judge Yu held a court hearing and sentenced Yao Atu to a fine of 400 yuan and Yao Shunfu to six months imprisonment and a fine of 200 yuan. However, since Yao Atu was unable to pay the fine, his sentence was converted to imprisonment at a rate of two yuan per day for six months and twelve days.

Robbery Alarm Outside Xiaobeimen: On the evening of the 5th, at about 8:00 PM, bandits numbering two to three hundred arrived at Zhangjia Village, Qinglong Township, north of the railroad outside Xiaobeimen, Wuyi County. The villagers, supporting the old and carrying the young, fled to the vicinity of Xiaobeimen. Upon receiving the news, the Fourth Sub-station of Public Security immediately telegraphed the County Public Security Bureau for instructions. While also sending police officers to stand guard. The Public Security Bureau dispatched the Wood Shell Team to assist in patrolling and discussed plans for suppression. At about 9:00 PM, the city gate of Xiaobeimen was closed, and temporary strict martial law was imposed in the Xinfeng Street area. The situation became tense for a time.

Bidding for Menghe and Canal Projects Simultaneously: Preparations for the dredging of the Menghe and Canal Rivers in Wuyi County are complete. The Menghe project is estimated to cost 170,000 yuan, and the Canal project is estimated to cost 300,000 yuan. The fundraising has also been decided. Therefore, the bidding period for Menghe is set from November 26 to December 10, and the bidding will open at the county government on the 11th. The bidding period for the canal is set from December 6 to the morning of the 15th, and the bidding will open at the Chamber of Commerce at 2:00 PM in the afternoon. Once a winning bidder is selected, the dam can be broken and construction can begin on a scheduled date.

Before long, the townspeople saw through their disguise and knew that they were not good people. They did not dare to talk to them. Within two days, the boat sailed into the sea.

Changes in the Fourth and Seventh District Chiefs: Zhu Qingnan, the Fourth District Chief of Shazhou, has served in his post for a year. In the past month, he has been repeatedly accused. Zhang Dada and acquaintances Wang Rongchao and Wu Ronggen got on the boat together when Zhang went to the city to wash seaweed. Zhang had secretly discussed robbing the boat. On the fifth day of the tenth lunar month in Changzhou, Zhang was seen to have received one yuan in profits. After the interrogation, he was sent to the city on the fourth day and after interrogation in the county, Ju confessed without reservation and court ordered him to be taken into custody and sentenced.

Aboard a Robbed Passenger Boat, Victim Dies Tragically: Pan Biliang, a grain merchant from Yitaiyuan Lu Chenhang outside the south gate of this city, loaded a boat with rice to sell at the Lu Chenhang. Yesterday (the 3rd) morning, after receiving the price, he took the original boat to Jiangba Town under the jurisdiction of Xuyi County to purchase miscellaneous grains. En route, when he arrived at Qiaojiajian in Huxi, he suddenly encountered a ship. Seven bandits suddenly appeared, each holding a gun, shouting to stop the boat. They swarmed onto the boat and immediately tied up Pan Biliang, stabbing him in the neck with a sharp blade, causing him to fall to the ground and die. They then dragged his son, Hongchun, out of the cabin and shot him to death. Subsequently, they searched the boat and stole 739 silver dollars, a self-defense pistol, and dozens of bolts of white cloth. His nephew, Pan Youhua, and the wife of the deceased have reported the incident to the county government, requesting a strict investigation. An absconded Provincial Public Security Team Captain: Pengfei, the captain of the 23rd Team of the 6th District of the Provincial Public Security Team stationed at the Fairy Temple, was reported to have uncovered a large-scale earthmoving operation established by the Yu family in Tangtou Town, Yangzhou in August of this year, and privately fined them a large sum of money. Subsequently, Xu Zijin, Zhou Zicheng, and Xu Chaoshan, merchants and farmers from Yangzhou, filed a complaint with the Civil Affairs Department. Zhenjiang

Yangzhong County Intercepts Construction Public Funds: Recently, citizens of Yangzhong County reported that County Magistrate Xu had intercepted and misappropriated construction public funds. The Construction Department sent the Construction Bureau Chief of Zhenjiang County to investigate. Yesterday, Chief Zhang returned to the province and found five instances of the county magistrate's interception: (1) When the county magistrate also served as the Finance Bureau Chief, tax collectors were short more than 1,800 yuan. Although the tax collectors Wang Zhaohong and Zhang Lijian have fully paid back the debt and redeemed the guarantee, the county magistrate has not turned over a single cent to the Construction Bureau for safekeeping. (2) The former Finance Bureau handed over the supplementary payments from tax collectors for various regular and special taxes in the 18th year of the Republic to the relevant parties for collection. However, more than 1,000 yuan in land tax for road construction was also intercepted. (3) The county magistrate misappropriated more than 1,490 yuan in special construction funds for administrative expenses and planned to repay the funds from the provincial tax revenue, starting in June, with priority given to repayment in the 19th year. However, the county has not allocated any funds since the collection began in May, which is hindering credibility. (4) The county's Finance Bureau was abolished and merged into the county government's Finance Section seven months ago, but there has been no regular accounting since then. As a result, the construction land tax of more than 1,000 yuan from the Lesheng Baojin Two Islands is impossible to investigate and collect, and more than 1,000 yuan in rent from the Lesheng Sancheng Island, which is a special fund for repairing the river embankment, is also difficult to investigate and collect. (5) The county magistrate ignored the Construction Department's important policies, and is suspected of ineffective collection of construction land tax in the 17th year of the Republic, which was supplemented this year. In addition, the collected funds are not being allocated.

In the Jiajia Lane Robbery Case, Both the Robbers and Goods Were Recovered: There was a robbery at Xia Liu's house at No. 44 Jiajia Lane the day before yesterday, resulting in the loss of silver dollars, clothing, ornaments, and miscellaneous items. At around 5:00 PM yesterday, detectives from the Public Security Bureau found three suspicious individuals at No. 12 Paiwantou Lane and immediately arrested them and brought them back for interrogation. One, Chen Lunyuan, 25 years old, from Suqian; one, Chen Niansen, 26 years old, from Hebei; and one, Wang Yuting, 39 years old, from Suqian, all confessed to robbing Xia Liu's house in Jiajia Lane. Most of the clothing and jewelry have now been recovered.

Proposed Reform of Consumption Tax: The Ministry of Finance previously established various special tax bureaus in the provinces as a preparation for abolishing likin. However, after a good is declared for tax, it can only circulate in one province, and it must be declared again in another province. The ministry is now preparing to reform the special consumption tax because the national government has explicitly ordered the abolition of likin on January 1. It has sent special personnel to investigate the provinces in order to start the reform. Jiang Chengsheng, the investigator sent by the Ministry of Finance to Jiangsu Province, arrived in the province yesterday and is scheduled to convene silk factories, lumber industries, oil industries, tea industries, pottery industries, and paper industries to speak today. It is heard that after the abolition of likin, it will still be difficult for taxed goods to circulate throughout the country. It is planned to first designate the six provinces of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Jiangxi, Hunan, and Hubei as a free circulation area and gradually expand it.

It is heard that he plans to inspect the 265th Regiment in Yangzhou at the Sheng Yang Middle School drill field by the Yangtze River tomorrow morning, and the 266th Regiment in the afternoon.

Verdict Announced in the Yanghuo Road Disaster Case: The Public Security Bureau's police force successively apprehended five suspects in connection with the worker riot that occurred in March of this year on Yanghuo Road in this county, in which construction bureau officials were beaten and injured. The suspects, Xia Guohuai, Xie Zhengfu, Shi Youfa, Xia Shaotang, and Wang Changsen, were sent to the court, which has held two hearings. It is now known that a verdict was announced yesterday (the 4th), and Xia Guohuai and the others were all acquitted.

Jiaxing

Notorious Opium Dealer Captured: Xiao Abing, a notorious opium dealer in Jiaxing, has repeatedly been hunted down by government officials, but always slipped through the net. Last year, after the county public security bureau seized a large amount of opium from him, they requested a warrant for his arrest. Recently, as the crackdown eased, Xiao secretly returned to Jiaxing to resume his old business. On the night of the 5th, someone informed the local court, and a prosecutor led police to capture Xiao and seize more than two liang of opium. Xiao was immediately taken to the court and placed in custody.

Huzhou

Series of Robberies in Minjiakan: Min Maosong, a farmer from Minjiakan, a place about ten li outside the Xiaodongmen in Changxing, Huzhou, lived a simple life, barely making ends meet. On the night of the 3rd, at about 10:00 PM, more than a dozen gangsters suddenly arrived, speaking in a Hakka accent and armed with guns. They broke down the door and robbed the house, taking all the clothes and silver. The gangsters then went to the neighboring Min family and rummaged through boxes and cabinets, searching at will. The losses of the two families amounted to more than 400 yuan. Court Courier Meets Thieves En Route: Shen Shigan, a court courier from the Wuxing branch in this city, took a boat to Ling on the 2nd to deliver official documents to the countryside. While passing through the Chefuyang area, he suddenly encountered a pirate ship. Two bandits shouted to stop the oars. The two bandits boarded the boat, threatened him into silence, and searched him at will. They stripped Shen of his clothes and robbed him of his official documents and silver dollars. After the robbery, the bandits returned to their original boat and sped away. It is heard that Shen immediately returned to Ling by the original boat and took a boat back to the source to report the incident and request assistance in the investigation.

Ningbo

Smugglers Beat Salt Police to Death: Xu Weiquan, the captain of the salt police team stationed in Sanqishi, Cixi, received a report from a secret agent that a large number of salt smugglers would be passing through Zhangting. After receiving the report, the captain dispatched police officer Cai Zaixiang, along with salt police Wang Tonglin, Zhou Youjian, Qian Zhangquan, and Lv Wenzhang, to Fangjiagang, ten li from Zhangting, on the afternoon of the 3rd to wait. At around 4:00 PM, they saw more than 50 smugglers each carrying a load of salt approaching. Salt policeman Wang Tonglin immediately stepped forward to question them. However, upon seeing the salt police, the smugglers, without asking questions, used shoulder poles to beat them indiscriminately, killing salt policeman Wang Tonglin and taking away the wooden holster that Wang was wearing. Seeing the unfavorable situation, the other salt police opened fire in self-defense, also wounding seven smugglers.

False Alarm of Thieves: Military and Police Surround Girls' School: At around 2:00 AM yesterday morning, when there was a fire under the Kuqiao Bridge in front of the Drum Tower in Ningbo, many hooligans used large stones to smash the gate of the Ningbo Dingxin Street Adult Women's School, intending to take advantage of the fire to rob the school. All the teachers and students of the school suspected that they were thieves and panicked. The school janitor used the telephone to call the military and police agencies for help. Soon, hundreds of military and police officers arrived, creating a very tense situation. Seeing this situation, the students became even more frightened. Subsequently, the school principal, Qiu Shenzhi, knew that the military and police had arrived. While reassuring the students, she informed the military and police that there were no thieves inside the school. The military and police chiefs then realized that the school janitor had mistakenly reported the theft alarm and severely reprimanded him. The military and police then dispersed, but many of the female students were still terrified.

Xiaoshan

Silt in Qiantang River Obstructs Traffic: Silt in the Qiantang River has blocked the river's flow. The Shaoxiao Yidu Steamboat cannot reach its destination directly. Each day, the journey upstream along the river from the Zhakou to the Liuhe Pagoda to one side, up to the Changhe Guanshan in Xiaoshan to the other, takes at least one or two hours longer. The Qiantang River is a vital artery for traffic between Hangzhou and Shaoxing. Recently, due to the silt in the river, traffic has been obstructed, and passengers are complaining.

To the Editor: I am directed to inform you that His Excellency the Chairman has instructed that a political news item carried by most newspapers in Beijing and Shanghai on December 4, which stated that the Executive Yuan would expand its organization to establish four departments, namely Secretariat, General Affairs, Political Affairs, and Councilors, was found to be untrue after investigation and verification. The news item should be corrected by letter to the various newspapers. Accordingly, I write to you to request that you check and correct the record. Respectfully, Civil Service Office of the National Government, December 5.

Letter from the 20th Army Liaison Office in Beijing

To the Editor: Our army's Lin and Yuan regiments fought a bloody battle with bandits in Huang'an for six days and nights. After the bandits were routed, they were ordered to return to Huanggang. En route, they were ambushed at night in Xinzhou by a bandit army division that detoured around the area. Outnumbered and outgunned, they suffered some losses. The situation regarding the arrival of reinforcements and pursuit of the bandits after they retreated has already been reported to headquarters by telegram. Your newspaper's claim that a certain unit of our army mutinied in Xinzhou is completely inconsistent with the facts. Please correct it immediately to avoid misunderstanding. Respectfully, 20th Army Liaison Office in Beijing, December 5, 19th year of the Republic, December 5.

Education News

Important News: Annual Meeting of the Chinese Society for Arts and Sciences (Part 2)

Paper Presentations: The fourth annual meeting of the Chinese Society for Arts and Sciences was held in Beijing. As reported yesterday, the meeting took place at the Biological Museum of National Central University on the morning of the 4th at 8:00 AM. All members attended, and a considerable number of people were present as observers. The important papers presented are disclosed below:

(1) Study of the Three Principles of the People (Lin Fu, read by Qiu Jingni)

(2) The Issue of Reducing Provincial Areas (Yang Donglin)

(3) On the Independence of Library Education (Ma Zongrong)

(4) Trends in Academic Learning during the Three Hundred Years of the Qing Dynasty (Chen Zhongfan)

(5) Changes in the Use of Words in Ancient Chinese Literature (Yang Yufu, read by Chen Zhongfan)

(6) Ancient Meanings of Several Terms (Chen Zhu, read by Chen Zhongfan)

(7) A Study on the History of Chinese Alchemy (Zheng Zhenwen)

(8) Superstitions in the Geological Community and Future Development Trends (Zhang Hongzhao)

(9) The Difference between the Ideal Gas Law and the Actual Experiments with Mixed Gases (Zhang Dingzhao)

(10) Approximate Components of *Salix psammophila* Produced in the Northeast (Zeng Guangfang)

(11) Biochemical Research on Wheat Flour (Tao Weisun)

(12) The Spreading of Filamentous Fungi in the Lower Reaches of the Yangtze River (Yin Benqiang)

(13) Experimental Research on Linear Amyloidosis (Go Shaolong)

(14) The Application of *Hengjing* Yeast (Wei Yanshou)

(15) The Absorption of Nitrates and Nucleic Acid by Higher Plants (Luo Zonglu)

(16) Chemical Research on the Mud of West Lake (Chen Zhilin)

(17) A Rapid Analytical Method for Lead Acetate (Han Zukang, Zhu Zili)

(18) Micro-Endpoint Titration Method (Han Zukang, Zhao Zongyu)

(19) A Study on the Sharp-Mouth Crab Species Produced in Southern China (Fei Hongnian)

(20) Production of Domestic Vitamins (Wang Zhaocheng)

Society Affairs Meeting: The society affairs meeting was held at 2:00 PM. Chairman Chuan Shi said the meeting would proceed as usual. First, the chairman reported that the fourth annual meeting should have been held earlier, but was delayed due to the influence of the current situation. There were many accumulated cases over the years, and actual work could not be fully achieved. At the Society Anniversary on the 17th year of the Republic, it was resolved to reorganize the society, re-register members, and elect officers according to the new charter. Accumulated cases were gradually cleared, and the society's work proceeded in an orderly manner. As a result, the construction of the society's office in Shanghai was actively promoted and it was decided to hold the fourth annual meeting in the capital this year. Fortunately, the construction is now largely completed and work can begin soon. Now that peace is restored within the country, the fourth annual meeting of the society is also being held in an atmosphere of unity after the Fourth Plenary Session. The Fourth Plenary Session paid attention to construction, and the society's annual meeting also focuses on the society's construction, so this annual meeting is very meaningful. The purpose of the society is (to study truth, promote learning, exchange knowledge, and promote culture), but the academic journals and series published are all personal research, and the promotion of culture has not been fully achieved. Special efforts should be made in the future. Subsequently, Executive Secretary Ma Zongrong reported that the society's registration procedures had been completed, and the office building contract had also been processed and construction could begin soon. The existing publications, including *Xueyi* (Learning) Magazine, *Xueyi* Paper Collection, *Xueyi* Series, *Xueyi Huikan* (Learning Miscellany), and *Wenyi* (Literary Arts) Series, will continue to be published as before. Ancient books that have been out of print and lost abroad, such as novels and operas from the Yuan and Ming dynasties, have already been successfully reprinted in several cases. It is planned to publish one hundred types of *Xueyi Huikan* and one hundred world-renowned works, some of which have already been published. In addition, it is planned to plan and issue socialized *Xueyi Wenku* (Learning Library) and Japanese language lectures, etc. There are also ways to introduce new domestic publications, which will be published monthly in the society's monthly report for scholars to refer to. Furthermore, the society's members are not biased towards one faction or system. Any intellectual in the country can be a member of the society to promote cultural movement. Next, Accountant Gao Shiguang reported on the financial situation, and Liu Shiying reported on the purchase of land and construction of the office. Then the proposals were discussed.

Banquet by the Ministry: After the meeting adjourned, the attendees went to the Ministry of Transportation for dinner. Minister Wang Boqun delivered a welcome speech, and everyone dispersed in joy around 10:00 PM.

Jiangsu Province Normal Education Achievement Exhibition Record

The Jiangsu Province Normal Education Achievement Exhibition was initiated by the Jiangsu Provincial Normal Science Federation with the purpose of (praising the spirit of normal education and arousing social attention to normal education). It was scheduled to be held at Yangzhou Middle School of Jiangsu Province on December 1st and 2nd, as reported earlier. It is now learned that the meeting has already been held with a total of fifteen exhibition rooms, including sixteen schools: Zhenjiang Middle School Normal School, Nanjing Middle School Normal School, Huaian Middle School Normal School, Suzhou Middle School Normal School, Wuxi Middle School Normal School, Tongzhou Middle School Normal School, Taizhou Middle School Normal School, Songjiang Girls' Middle School Normal School, Suzhou Girls' Middle School Normal School, Shanghai Middle School Normal School, Yangzhou Middle School Normal School, Xiangfu Middle School Xiangfu Normal School, Shanghai Middle School Xiangfu Normal School, Wuxi Middle School Xiangfu Normal School, Yangzhou Middle School Xiangfu Normal School, and Nanjing Middle School Suzhou Normal School. Each school's exhibits were divided into three categories: administrative achievements, academic achievements, and extracurricular activity achievements. The achievements were extremely rich, and the visitors were very enthusiastic. Moreover, each school's achievements had its advantages, such as Taizhou Middle School's Party Ideology Wall Chart, Nanjing Middle School's administrative forms, Shanghai Middle School's original Living Research Wall Chart, health education materials, natural history specimens, and the Education Research Association's publications, Yangzhou Middle School's entire design of a small school, Tongzhou Middle School's design of an ideal school, Suzhou Middle School's elementary school Chinese language materials, Suzhou Girls' Middle School's Chinese language and arithmetic teaching aids, Songjiang Girls' Middle School's arithmetic teaching aids, Wuxi Middle School's plant specimens, Zhenjiang Middle School's educational propaganda wall chart, Shanghai Middle School Xiangfu Normal School's three-year agricultural experiment report and art teaching aids, Suzhou Middle School Xiangfu Normal School's physics and chemistry teaching aids, Wuxi Middle School Xiangfu Normal School's teaching materials for various subjects, Nanjing Middle School Xiangfu Normal School's farm photography, Yangzhou Middle School Xiangfu Normal School's self-made physics equipment, and Huaian Middle School's handicraft achievements. All of these were sufficient to represent the spirit of normal education and serve as a reference for other provinces to run normal education.

This Municipality's Municipal Education Bureau Orders Municipal Schools to Report Free Students by a Deadline

Before the 20th of this month

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau issued an instruction yesterday to the municipal schools, stating that some students in municipal schools who have requested exemption from tuition fees and construction fees have not submitted their requests to the bureau for approval in accordance with the regulations. At the end of this semester, if there are any students in each school who must request free admission, they should submit their requests in accordance with the regulations before the 20th of this month and fill out the free student report form to apply for approval. Applications submitted after the deadline will not be accepted. They must comply with this order.

Jiangnan University Football Tournament

Jiaotong University defeated Guanghua 4-1

Jinan University defeated Zhonggong 9-1

—Match between Jiaotong University and Guanghua—

The Jiangnan University Championship match between the football teams of Guanghua and Jiaotong Universities was held at Xujiahui at 2:30 PM yesterday. As a result, Jiaotong University defeated Guanghua 4-1. There were many spectators around, and both sides cheered with cheerleaders and various slogans, making it a grand occasion.

In the first half, Guanghua was in a precarious situation and could barely defend, let alone attack. Jiaotong University's surprise attacks were very intense. Jiaotong University won 2-0. In the second half, Guanghua showed some promise and the situation was slightly balanced, resulting in a score of 4-1. The strength of the two teams was originally very evenly matched. Fudan had tied Jiaotong University 1-1, and Guanghua had defeated Fudan 2-1. However, Jiaotong University defeated Guanghua 4-1, showing how unpredictable the outcome is. Guanghua was unfamiliar with the grass field, and the grass field was slippery after the rain, making them even more unable to perform, resulting in a crushing defeat. Referee: Yue Xiurong.

The competition was fierce, and both sides had opportunities but failed to score. At 27 minutes, Liu Ximeng, the center forward of Jiaotong University, opened the scoring. This ball was scored from more than ten yards away. Jiaotong University students cheered, and everyone far and near heard it. After this loss, Guanghua's morale was lost and, unfortunately, disaster struck. Four minutes later, they lost another goal. This ball was crossed by Fei Fuxu of Jiaotong University, and Wan Mian made a diagonal shot. The Guanghua inside defense was caught off guard, and Liu Ximeng of Jiaotong University took the opportunity to jump forward and put the ball in. The first half ended 2-0.

At the start of the second half, Guanghua was still mostly defending and rarely attacking. Zhang Jinrong of Jiaotong University also scored a goal. Under this heavy blow, Guanghua had to cheer up and try to counterattack. The Jiaotong University goal was in danger. Yang Renwei of Guanghua made a solo attack and passed the difficult situation. Seeing that the opportunity was ripe, he kicked the ball into the net. Guanghua students cheered for a while. Jiaotong University then launched a major attack. In the last five minutes, Fei Fuxu of Jiaotong University dribbled the ball and sent it to the front of the Guanghua goal. Wan Mian headed the ball into the goal in the chaos. As a result, Jiaotong University won 4-1. The lineups of the two sides are as follows:

—Match between Jinan and Zhonggong—

The Jiangnan University Football Championship match between Jinan and Zhonggong was held in Wusong at 2:30 PM yesterday. Zhonggong's football skills have improved a lot in recent years, but Jinan is famous at home and abroad. Even though Chen Jiaqiu and Jiang Shanjing and others are participating in the Zhongzi group competition of the Chinese Association, their strength is still strong. As a result, they defeated Zhonggong 9-1. Referee: He Chunhui.

The field was uneven, and the ground was wet after the rain, making it difficult to play. In the first half, Jinan scored two goals first, and Zhonggong retaliated with only two. In the second half, Jinan's offensive became stronger, and Zhonggong had almost no resistance. Jinan scored one goal after another. As a result, the score was 9-1. Jinan was penalized once for a penalty kick. Zhonggong kicked it in, but before they kicked it, another ball had already run into the penalty area, so it was re-kicked and blocked by goalkeeper Liang Guanlian. After the game, Zhonggong offered tea and refreshments, and the hosts and guests dispersed in joy. The lineups of the two sides are as follows:

Far Eastern Games Records

Will Be Recognized as Official Records

Japanese Athletic Meet Scheduled to Be Determined

Tokyo News from the World News Agency: The All-Japan Athletic Federation recently recognized the track and field records of the Ninth Far Eastern Championships. The International Athletic Federation has now received a notice from the Federation that if the Japanese Sports Committee decides to recognize them, there is no objection to them being recognized as official records. Therefore, the Japanese Athletic Federation will hold a sports committee on December 13 to decide on its attitude.

Special Investigation Committee Dispatched by the Chinese National Sports Association to Investigate the Qualifications of Yuehua Football Team Members

Did Not Violate Amateur Rules

Yu Hengzhi Should Report Accounts

—Investigation Results Have Been Submitted to the Board of Directors for Judgment——

Regarding the issue of the amateur status of members of the Yuehua Football Team, the Board of Directors of the Chinese National Sports Association specifically dispatched three members, Shen Siliang, Huang Mingdao, and Zhao Jinqing, to conduct a special investigation. The investigation by the committee has now concluded and has been submitted to the Board of Directors for judgment. Because the directors are busy with official duties, there is no date set for a meeting. Therefore, the report and the International Amateur Sports Regulations will be published in the newspaper to satisfy the desire of all parties. The resolution of the Board of Directors will be disclosed after it is decided at the meeting. The report, etc., are recorded below.

Report on the Amateur Status Review of the Lehua Football Team

The Lehua Football Team is a Chinese amateur sports organization. Because there was suspicion that some of its members were not amateurs, the National Sports Federation of China appointed a special committee to investigate the matter to clarify the truth.

I. This committee was specially appointed by the Board of Directors of the National Sports Federation of China.

II. This committee is an independent organization responsible for investigating the situation of this case and submitting a responsible report to the Board of Directors of the National Sports Federation of China.

III. The duty of this committee is specifically to review the amateur status of the members of the Lehua Sports Association's expedition football team organized this year.

(Committee Meeting)

This committee has held several meetings and, on November 12, 1920, at 4:00 PM, questioned the officers and members of the Lehua Football Team at the Shanghai Bankers' Association. The detailed report of the findings is as follows:

I. The team's expedition was initiated by several people and organized under the name of the Lehua Sports Association.

II. The team did not obtain formal approval from the National Sports Federation of China and the Shanghai Football Association.

III. The team initially used the name "(Lehua)" for the expedition and later changed it to "(Chinese Expedition Team)."

IV. Players and organizers did not sign contracts.

V. An Englishman, Harris, was responsible for making contacts in England.

VI. The Englishman, Li Silian, was hired as a supervisor and correspondence secretary.

VII. It was agreed that each match would be subsidized by the host team to cover expenses.

VIII. Players were not consulted about the team's financial situation.

IX. Financial matters were managed by Yu Hengzhi, a representative of the Lehua Sports Association and the team's manager.

X. Each player received a daily allowance of two yuan (local silver dollars).

XI. The Lehua Sports Association provided each player with football equipment and a set of evening dress worth up to 250 yuan.

XII. Players did not provide receipts for the daily allowance, but receipts were issued for the evening dress expenses and are pending verification.

XIII. Yu Hengzhi had full authority over the funds of the Lehua Sports Association.

XIV. Yu Hengzhi has not yet reported the accounts to the Lehua Sports Association (because the accounts for match revenue from various locations have not been settled).

XV. The financial situation of this trip was quite satisfactory.

XVI. The trip to Europe was canceled due to a telegram from London advising against it.

XVII. The original planned duration of the overseas trip was eight months.

XVIII. The actual duration of the overseas trip was three months.

Conclusion

(I) According to the report of the 9th Far Eastern Games (published by the National Sports Federation of China, page 17) and the amateur rules of the International Football Federation, the players of the team have not violated any rules.

(II) This committee recommends that Yu Hengzhi report the accounts to the Lehua Sports Association as soon as possible.

Recommendations

I. This committee recommends that the National Sports Federation appoint a dedicated committee to investigate the domestic situation in detail and formulate amateur sports rules for national compliance.

II. This committee further recommends that it be announced that any Chinese sports organizations planning to compete abroad should first obtain approval from the Sports Federation. Those who do not have such procedures should be subject to strict review.

Special Investigation Committee, November 14, 1920

Attached Amateur Sports Rules

(I) Amateur athletes may not participate in non-amateur sports competitions.

(II) Amateur athletes may not accept salaries or compensation for losses.

Attached Definition of Amateur Sports by the International Football Federation

Article 1 The Federation is in charge of cultivating amateur sports and governing professional football.

Article 2 Athletes are divided into amateur and professional.

Article 4 An athlete who receives money or clothing expenses or travel expenses exceeding legitimate expenses shall be considered a professional athlete.

Article 6 Amateur athletes who receive money should provide special receipts. These receipts must be available for review by the National Sports Federation and the Federation at any time.

Article 8 An athlete who participates in competitions for monetary prizes is a professional athlete.

Article 9 When a sports governing body declares an athlete to be a professional athlete, the athlete loses his amateur status.

Article 10 Clubs affiliated with the Federation and its member associations, regardless of whether the athletes in the club are amateurs or not, may not derive economic benefits from managing or subsidizing the club's finances.

Article 11 An athlete who sells or manages sports goods is not considered a professional athlete.

Article 12 Amateur athletes are absolutely not allowed to use their names or football reputation for advertising or proprietary advertising purposes.

Article 13 Amateur athletes are not allowed to use their photographs for commercial advertising purposes.

Article 13 (A) The period for a professional athlete to regain amateur status is one full year (from the date of application to the National Sports Federation). During this one full year, the athlete must completely disassociate himself from professional sports. An athlete who engages in professional sports a second time can never regain amateur status.
