Free Talk

Take it with a Grain of Salt

— Sea Guest

Mistress (to the new maid): From today onwards, you will be working for us, and you must obey our every command.

Maid: Madam, I know, and I would never dare to act on my own accord.

Mistress: I am not someone who likes to talk much. If I raise my hand, it means I am calling you over.

Maid: I am also not someone who likes to talk much. If I shake my head, it means I do not want to come over.

Hotel Waiter (entering a room with many rowdy young men): Please, gentlemen, be quiet. The old gentleman next door has reported to the accounting office that your nightly disturbances are so loud that he cannot concentrate on his reading.

One Young Man: Go tell him that if he cannot concentrate on his reading, he should be ashamed of himself for even bringing it up. We were able to read the Three Character Classic and the Hundred Family Surnames when we were five or six years old.

Old Gentleman (looking at several wine bottles with disgust, speaking to a young man): How can you young people all love this stuff? What is the pleasure of getting drunk and senseless? I am already sixty years old and have never had a sip of alcohol.

Young Man: Poor old man, you have lived your entire life for nothing, not even experiencing some simple pleasures. You do not have much time left in this world. Have a glass now.

Doctor (on his rounds in the hospital, asking a nurse in one of the patient rooms): How is this patient? Is his heart condition improving?

Nurse: Much better. Since last night, he has proposed to me three times.

Interesting News from the Japanese Depression

— Wang Yanjin

During the European War, Western countries were preoccupied with military affairs and had no time for trade. The Far Eastern market was dominated by Japan. The capital of merchants suddenly increased, and the national economy became prosperous. Commentators called it the Golden Age of Japan, and the Japanese themselves called it "Upper Boom." However, extreme prosperity must decline. The more developed capitalism is, the greater the risk of overproduction. In recent years, the number of unemployed has increased, causing a great economic panic. The Japanese call it the Depression. In this era of depression, everything is being rationalized, so there are many good stories recorded in this discussion, which can be used to understand the Japanese countryside.

Rationalization of Marriage. Tokyo newspapers have published numerous articles about the rationalization of marriage. Because Japanese rural areas are widely troubled by the severe depression, rural men and women are thus inclined to rationalize marriage and greatly save on marriage costs. This is indeed a good story in the era of depression. The women's association of Tanio Village, Mie Prefecture, contributed three corners of gold each to make a complete set of wedding clothes for members to borrow and wear for marriage. It is said that since the set of wedding clothes was made, twelve new couples have borrowed and worn them for marriage. Among them, there are new couples who borrowed and wore them for the fourth time, and they are not very harmonious with each other. The sound of the Japanese reading (four) is like (death), which is suspected to be a bad omen, so they are depressed. In Isozawa Village, Fukushima Prefecture, the wedding ceremony, including the banquet, is not allowed to take more than two hours. Also, the women's youth group of Ichinichi Town, Akiyama Prefecture, jointly produced 93 yuan of sweat and blood money to make a wedding dress. Whenever a member is about to get married, they will wear this dress for marriage. However, November 8th was the wedding date of the three group members, and they competed with each other for this dress, almost to the point of fighting. Later, the group leader borrowed it from another village, and the matter was resolved.

Rationalization of Reading. There are three elementary schools in the village of Sengokuiwa, Nagasaki Prefecture. The students in the school are mostly children from farming families and are severely affected by the depression. Therefore, the teachers of each school jointly formed an elementary school farm, where they plant vegetables after school every day for living and for lunch at school (most of the students in Sengokuiwa Village's elementary schools are day students and send their lunch to school). In the past, the monthly cost of lunch was seven yuan, but now it is only five yuan. It is said that from April next year, students in the second grade and above in the village's elementary school will have to hand-copy textbooks to save costs and facilitate memorization.

A Test Ride on a Ford Airplane in Beijing on November 17

— Yang Xingfu

Long-suffering without wings in a towering city,

Suddenly soaring against the wind each day.

City walls seem like footprints in the sand,

The people are originally poor worms.

Why transform into a crane and lament the past?

Already seen the cosmic dust transforming into empty space.

If emptiness could last forever,

Humans should not lament the end of the road.

Tune: Huan Xi Sha

— Liu Xuanque

Returning Home Late in the Capital

The dusk city walls seem dyed with rouge,

Snow on the mountain peaks still scattered.

In this cold season, who cherishes the flowers?

The carriage wheels run over the hills, like a dream,

The deep color of tea in the cup, complaining of affection.

The meeting of man and heaven is always difficult to predict.

Footprints cover the dust, tears stain the clothes,

The blue sky is silent, facing the clear light.

The misty rain is easy to capture in photos,

Sorrowful, only worrying about the lamp obstructing the moon.

Drifting and scattered, I fear my hair will turn to silk,

Each winding stream resembles a beautiful eyebrow.

Record of the 29th Anniversary Celebration of the Patriotic Girls' School

— Yu Jianhua

The Patriotic Girls' School is the oldest girls' school in Shanghai, now in its 29th year. The old site in Tianbao Lane was too small, so this autumn, it was moved to Chenyuan on Jiangwan Road, where the flowers and trees are beautiful, making it a great place to study. Unfortunately, the buildings are still not enough, so this year's celebration was held at the school because the auditorium could not accommodate many people, and a grand celebration will be held next year for the 30th anniversary. This year, it was only held at the school for the teachers and students to enjoy. The anniversary ceremony was held on the morning of the second. Director Qu Sun Xiangzhong reported, and Mr. Zhang Shiaoan, the author, and students gave speeches, all of which were a mix of seriousness and humor, and there was thunderous applause. In the afternoon, there was the volleyball championship final, and in the evening, there was a variety of performances, which started at 6:30 PM and ended at 12:30 AM. There were thirty programs in total, including dances such as "Spring Comes to the World," a four-person dance, "Butterfly Love Flower," "Butterfly Girl," "Spring Breeze's Favor," "Flower Selling Song," "Mother's Heart," "Crane Matchmaker Dance," "Grasshopper and Bee," "Echo Dance," "Venus Descends," and "Little Painter," with clear songs and beautiful dances emerging one after another. In Beijing opera, Lei Zemin, Bai Lizhen, Shi Xiuwen, and alumna Ms. Lu won the most applause. The new dramas included "Sacrifice," "Temporary Friend," "Tragedy on the Lake," "Absolute Break," and "Suzhou Night Talk," advocating male rights, with "Suzhou Night Talk" being the most brilliant. At the painful parts of the performance, many viewers had tears in their eyes, and even the author could not bear to finish listening. The alumna Ms. Jin Guangmei could not even look up, showing how deeply moved she was. "Advocating Male Rights" was a comedy written by the author, because as a result of advocating women's rights, women's rights have become increasingly important and male rights have become increasingly light. Two hundred years later, it will be the opposite of today's phenomenon, with men becoming slaves to women and being severely abused. Therefore, men plot a revolt in secret and hold a meeting, but it is discovered by women, and each wife reports her husband's ear, which can make the viewers laugh. Because guests were not invited that day, uninvited guests were refused, and armed police were specially invited to guard the gate, so no less than a hundred people from nearby schools who came in high spirits left in disappointment. On this day, the Patriotic Wall Newspaper specially published a commemorative special issue with as many as two hundred pages, about fifty to sixty thousand characters, completely filling the wall, and attached twelve flower and bird paintings by Ms. Wang Mingfen, which were also elegant and pleasing. The author has served at the Patriotic Girls' School and has encountered three commemorative meetings. I respectfully wish this girls' school, which is ten years older than the Republic of China, increasing glory and sharing prosperity with the country, then the author will also share in the honor.

The Crab Disaster

— Yan Qian

Bi Zhuo, the Personnel Officer of Jin, had the saying, "Holding a wine cup in the right hand and a crab claw in the left hand, floating on a wine boat is enough for a lifetime." The praise for crabs has reached its extreme. Now, the author alone wants to expose its crimes, or perhaps will be accused of being unreasonable because of this. However, if readers can benefit from this in the slightest, then that is my greatest wish.

Venerating Women. My relative, Madam Shen, suddenly suffered from abdominal pain one evening, and it gradually improved after four days and nights. It is said that the pain was very severe, like giving birth to a child. However, the cause of this was not only unknown to the patient, but even the doctor had no definite diagnosis. After a few more days, Ms. Zhu came as a guest and asked in surprise why Madam was ill. Madam replied that she had suffered from a strange disease. Ms. Zhu asked again for details and exclaimed, "If you ate crabs during your period, then it is the crab's fault." It turns out that the tenant in my family's厢楼楼 ate crabs when her period came, and that night, she suffered from severe abdominal pain, which only subsided after three or four days. Madam suddenly realized, "Could it be that my illness is also because of this?"

Killing Old Partners. A person from the countryside once told me that a diarrhea epidemic was prevalent in Puyuan Town at the end of last month, all caused by eating drunken crabs. A 58-year-old man surnamed Huai, who worked in a used clothing store, bought and ate drunken crabs, and that night, he had diarrhea thirty or forty times, and the next morning, he died. Initially, the old man Huai was talking and laughing happily after a full meal, but he never expected to lose his life because of the crabs. Therefore, the Jiaxing authorities temporarily banned the sale of drunken crabs, and those who sold them privately were given a light punishment. The narrator also said that he still remembered ten years ago, a town in the northern countryside of Jiaxing also caused a disease due to crabs, and both a relative and a friend suffered from the disaster. However, the author believes that drunken crabs cause illness or even death because the crabs happen to be sick or there are flaws in the drunkenness. It is not that all drunken crabs can harm people. Readers are wise and will definitely understand this.

Devouring Rice. Ancient records have the term "crab disaster," which refers to the harm that crabs do to crops in the fields. The Pingjiang Records says, "In the Dading Dingwei period, the crab disaster in Wuzhong was like locusts, filling the fields and devouring all the rice." Dading Dingwei was the eleventh year of the reign of Emperor Chengzong Temuer of the Yuan Dynasty, which was 623 years ago. Also, today's coastal areas are mostly inhabited by pengqi, which are similar to crabs. They burrow into the ground and damage dikes, which are also a major enemy of farmers.

Short News. The painter Wang Yachen and his wife, Ms. Rong Junli, have returned to China for more than a month. Li Shizeng, Cai Yuanpei, Yang Xingfu, Jiang Menglin, and the Shanghai Institute of Literature and Art have initiated a painting exhibition at the China Club at No. 150 Weihaiwei Road, Shanghai, starting on the 5th of this month and continuing for fourteen days. The exhibition will be held in eight rooms and will be divided into two types: original creations and reproductions of famous European works from various eras. All are welcome to visit without tickets. It is also said that exquisite catalogs will be distributed to visitors.

Travels in Southeast Asia (92)

— Ling Hua

From observing this, one can understand that Burma was once a tributary state of our dynasties, lost only for a few decades. Therefore, although the Burmese are not entirely in harmony with the Chinese, they are generally better than the treacherous English. Regarding political, geographical, and historical traces, Master Daogai traveled throughout Burma for one or two years and has notes that are of great evidentiary value. The northeastern border of Burma is at the confluence of Simao and Tengyue in Yunnan, bordering India and near Bhutan. If China unites and expands outward with the people of Guangxi and Yunnan, assisting the independence of Annam and Burma from French and English control, it would be a major issue. There are already many Chinese within Siam, Burma, and Annam. Half of the Siamese people have already mixed with the Chinese. The Siamese ruler also acknowledges that the expansion of the Chinese ethnic group's influence in Southeast Asia and the Asian Southeast is only a matter of time, and its potential has already been consolidated. It is a pity that the Chinese do not emphasize self-governance, lack connection, and have too small a vision. In the past, Annam paid tribute to us every two years, Siam every three years, and Burma every ten years. Now that external shackles have been completely removed and internal chaos is rampant, it is truly regrettable that the people do not quickly unite on economic self-governance to become powerful in East Asia. When talking with Burmese gentlemen, their hopes are deeply placed on us, and I am very grateful for their righteousness. Fifty miles away from Rangoon, there is a place called Pegu, said to be where Zhuge Liang arrived when he captured Meng Huo. The Burmese still worship Zhuge Liang today.

The soil of Burma is thick and fertile, originally the richest in the world. Its rice grains are long and fragrant. Master Daofa traveled throughout Burma and observed in great detail. He says there is a type of rice with four hundred grains per stalk. Someone ate rice in central Burma and said there was something special about it, and it was once presented as tribute to the king, truly the finest rice in the world. It yields multiple harvests a year and produces precious stones, pearls, jade, and teak wood. After the English obtained the land, they levied tens of millions in tax from Burma annually to be paid to England, provided 20 million as a subsidy to India, and used 40 million to govern the Burmese province. In total it collected 90 million, and various businesses absorbed its essence abroad, hence Burma is poor. The Burmese resent the English and therefore also resent the various overseas Chinese who trade with them. They have never ceased to harbor the sentiment of the Boxer Rebellion to eliminate them all in one fell swoop, but they lack the strength. As for why they demand separate governance from India, it is because they do not understand the 20 million going to India. However, the English are also very happy for Burma and India to separate governance because they fear that they will conspire to plot against us and unite in resistance, so they use many methods to cause division.

Warmth in the Heart (330)

— Bao Tianxiao

Chapter Sixteen: Cordial Inquiry for Characters, Emerald Sleeves Visit the Teacher; Generous Discussion of Military Affairs, Brothel Banquet with Heroic Women

A-Su said, “I think in summer, it doesn’t matter. We are used to wearing slippers barefoot in hot weather. But in winter, even though we still wear very thin silk stockings, the shoes outside are still velvet-faced and lined with felt. Taking off our shoes and walking on the cold, icy floor, we naturally feel unaccustomed. And there are some people who don’t really want people to see their feet.” As she spoke, she pointed to Luyi, saying, “Like our sister here, she also has natural feet that haven’t been bound. But when she washes her feet, she still closes the door of the small room and doesn’t allow anyone to enter.” Luyi and Zuo Shichen were originally talking about something, but after hearing A-Su’s words, she turned her head and said, “Sister, how can you talk about washing feet on the table?” A-Su laughed and said, “Fourth Young Master and Second Young Master are all family, what’s so important about talking about it?” Long Ziyun said, “You two sisters need to balance things out a bit. One sister is too talkative, and the other is too quiet.” Lin Fanzhi said, “Just now, they were called a good match.” A-Su said, “It’s good, but it’s a pity that we’ll be splitting up soon.” Zuo Shichen said, “What? Are you not in A-Su’s place next season?” It turned out that Luyi was contracted to A-Su’s mother. Zuo Shichen had known this for a long time. The brothel system in Shanghai, for those girls, besides buying them outright to be slaves, there were also two types of arrangements: debt bondage and seasonal contracts. Debt bondage could last for eight or ten years. Imagine a girl being forced into a brothel at the age of thirteen, and only being able to redeem herself at the age of twenty-three. A woman’s golden years would be completely ruined. Or maybe she would marry someone halfway through, which would be like escaping the fire pit of the brothel, but perhaps she would fall into the fire pit of a family. That was also a common occurrence. In short, the suffering of debt bondage was similar to that of being a slave. As for seasonal contracts, it was just contracting for one or two seasons, almost like a form of employment. The treatment was mostly courteous. After the contract expired, they would still return to their original owner. Moreover, if they were contracted by a young master, they would still return to them. The young master had the intention of Lin Xiangru returning the jade intact to Zhao. There were also many owners who didn’t trust the contractor, fearing that they would entice guests to secretly return to their small rooms every night. Now, hearing A-Su say that she was going to split up with Luyi soon, it must be that the term was up and she was no longer renewing the contract. Zuo Shichen then asked, “Where will you be next season?” But Luyi still looked at A-Su and refused to say. A-Su said, “Let me tell you. Next season, she’ll be opening her own room in Little Flower Garden, named Green Ripple. Sister, do you have a small picture to give to Second Young Master?” Luyi looked very embarrassed and said, “I didn’t bring my small picture.” A-Su said, “Don’t blame her for picking up customers. Where you are, Second Young Master will definitely be able to find you.”

Commercial News

Financial and Gold Market, Leaping Like Rabbits and Swooping Like Hawks

Difficult to Predict After Initial Fall and Subsequent Rise: Yesterday's Gold Market Situation. The situation was chaotic, with initial falls followed by rises, sudden jumps and falls, making it extremely difficult to predict. The overall trend could not be suppressed, with transactions revolving around two to three taels. However, towards the end, the momentum sharpened, with fluctuations of as much as eight taels in half a day. Trading houses were enthusiastic in their buying, such as Yuan Heng, Fu Chang, Xie Yu, and Zhifeng Yong, all aggressively chasing the price. However, the Ningbo banks, such as Tai Chenrun, mostly sold off. Overseas silver markets saw declines in London silver prices, but New York silver prices remained stable, causing gold prices to rapidly decline. However, the market was very chaotic, with prices rising and falling sharply. Later, as foreign exchange rates showed signs of easing and rumors spread about an earthquake in Japan, prices suddenly fell to 607.5 taels. Most foreign exchange rates rebounded by half a point, leading to further fluctuations around 610 taels. Subsequently, as exchange rates strengthened again and local buying became more intense, prices rose steadily, climbing by five taels and breaking through 615 taels. Short sellers panicked and could only cover their positions in the end at around 616 taels. In the afternoon, due to the Saturday market closure, the price fell by ten taels. The opening price for January was 608.7 taels, a decrease of 3.7 taels (the gross spread was around 8 to 10 taels, with buyers dominating). The recent decline in large bars was 1/8 for near-term and 1/16 for far-term, and with no sellers from the United States, sentiment was agitated, leading to a lower opening. Soon after, Yuan Heng, Fuchang, and others rushed to buy, jumping by more than three taels to 12.4 taels. Afterwards, there were fluctuations of one or two taels, but the sentiment was negative. Just over ten minutes later, prices crashed by more than four taels to 607.5 taels at 9:25 AM, with strong selling pressure. Almost simultaneously, the foreign exchange market also weakened. Mitsui bought 1.3 yuan per tael of Japanese gold for the current month, then divided it into 1.25 taels. Afterwards, the current price was only 1.34 taels. When the bill of exchange was announced, Yong Heng, Yuan Heng, Xie Yu, and others bought in, pushing the price back up by two taels to 10.03 to 11 taels. However, the listed exchange rate was increased to 1.25 US dollars, and the 25th Japanese gold fell by 875, which had no impact. The internal market remained stable. Sumitomo absorbed 1.63125 British gold in February. Before long, Dadecheng came to sell, and Korea offered 1.63125 British gold in March, resulting in a drop of two taels. At 9:30, the price was 608.89 taels. Then, Shanghai absorbed 1.6375 in March. The Mack Line bought 37.0625 yuan in US dollars for January. Yuan Heng and others continued to drag in goods on the floor, reaching 11.8 taels around 10:00 AM. After this, the ups and downs were complex, fluctuating by more than one tael. There was a momentary increase in sellers, and Japanese gold was traded among banks for 1.3 yuan in January. By 10:50 AM, it had fallen to 0.098 taels. After 11:00 AM, Zhifeng Yong, Jintai Yong, and Yuan Heng suddenly bought in heavily, so by 11:30 AM, the price was 13.4 taels. In an instant, it shed 1.5 taels to 12 taels. Sentiment was unsettled, and deposits and withdrawals were in disarray.

The evening market rebounded by 3.6 taels. After 1:15 PM, there was a sudden surge, with Zhifeng Yong, Xie Yu, Yuan Da Yong, and others buying aggressively, pushing the price up by more than two taels. Rumors circulated that a certain bank had bought cash, but this was not accurate. It was merely market hype. At the noon close, the price was 615.6 taels, an increase of 3.6 taels compared to the previous day. It then rose again to 16 taels. Market sentiment was extremely strong. The highest price for half a day was 15.6 taels, and the lowest price was 7.5 taels (referring to the listed price), a difference of 8.1 taels. Goods were priced at 8.7 taels in the morning and 16 taels at the noon close. The posted price has been changed to 653.8 taels. The Japanese gold listing has decreased by 875 initially, 43 taels internally later 45 taels was 38 taels at noon.

Transactions between traders were made hastily and hastily withdrawn. Trading was recorded between Yuan Heng, Fu Chang, Xie Yu, Yongfeng, Jin Da Yong, Yong Heng, Yuan Mao Yong, Zhifeng Yong, and goods progressed smoothly. Tai Kang Run, Kun He, and Tong Tai Chang etc. are all out Wanxing, Bingxing, Dadecheng and other came in and out for a short time. The Dalian Gang traded a total of 1,500 bars, while taking out 6 or 700 bars.

Foreign Exchange Weakens Before Strengthening

Yesterday, the overseas silver market saw continued declines in British silver, while US silver remained stable, making the market more calm. Exchange rates rose slightly. HSBC's listed prices suddenly increased by half a point, likely due to the easing market conditions in Shanghai. The British exchange rate rose to 1.125, currently at 1 shilling 6 pence 0.125. US dollars rose by 0.25 to 36.625 yuan. Indian exchange rates increased by 0.75 to 101.75 rupees. French francs increased by 7 yuan to 933 yuan. Japanese yen increased by 0.75 to 91 taels. German exchange rates increased by 1 yuan to 153 marks. Vietnamese exchange rates decreased by 1 tael to 152.25 taels. Hong Kong exchange rates remained unchanged at 80.075 taels. Youth Garden

French Student Zou Fusong Discovers Salt to Treat Skin Diseases and Electricity to Raise Fish and Plant

Seawater Fish Can Become Freshwater Fish

French student Zou Fusong conducted experiments at the Saint-Louis National Hospital in Paris to treat skin diseases with salt and found remarkable results. He found it effective for severe scrotal eczema that caused unbearable itching, for which Westerners' medicines were ineffective. After repeated experiments, Zou first washed the area with hot water for half a minute, then rubbed it with fine salt without any pain. Then, he washed it clean with hot water and rubbed it with fine salt again. He did this two or three times for a total of about five or six minutes. After that, he washed it clean with hot water and wiped it dry. He could do this continuously for three days (only once a day). This method is very simple and painless. It does not require electricity or medicine. Mild cases can be cured once or twice, and severe cases, even old diseases of more than ten years, will definitely be completely cured three or four times. This method can also be used for people without skin diseases. The entire scrotum can be rubbed with fine salt and hot water according to the method to cause heat and increase blood flow. Anyone, especially athletes or those returning from long journeys and feeling tired, can benefit from this method.

According to Zou's research, for all ringworm and any skin diseases on the whole body, after rubbing, washing, and drying with the above method, the area should be rubbed with a purple electric light emitter for about ten to fifteen minutes (depending on the size of the area). Ringworm on the scrotum does not need electricity. After using the method, the whole body heals quickly and the mind is clear.

Zou also has new inventions regarding raising fish with electricity, planting with electricity (motors), turning seawater fish into freshwater fish, turning freshwater fish into seawater fish, and various agricultural science inventions. Zou will also send these for publication and announce them to various countries in Paris.

The director and physicians of the Saint-Louis National Hospital in France are very satisfied with Zou's recent inventions and improvements and have applied the methods. The French in Paris said that Japan has Zou. Zou replied that he is Chinese, but Westerners said that China does not have this kind of science, and they ultimately did not believe it. Now they are gradually believing it and will be faster. Zou is scheduled to return to China in early December.

About the Fudan Xisheng Society

— Bin

This semester, Fudan's well-known wall newspaper tide has surged like waves again. Since the beginning of the semester, nearly a dozen wall newspapers such as Shortwave Radio, Purple Dove, Minchao, Brilliant, and Anti-Dawn have been published. Among them, the most colorful and the most noteworthy for the authorities is the Xisheng Society's (Xisheng), which is published on schedule and has never been delayed. It is published every three days and its content is extremely rich. It has accurate commentary, interesting East Palace Chronicles, agile news about the school authorities, and rigorous critical writing. Because its most successful step is to estimate the decline of proletarian literature based on the future trend and objective needs of the Chinese literary world, and to analyze the inside story of proletarian writers with precise eyes. These, since being published on Xisheng, have aroused the sympathy of the general students. From this, it can be seen that proletarian literature has only a very short history in the Chinese literary world and then comes to an end, which is also an inevitable phenomenon. The reason why the Xisheng wall newspaper can become the most powerful in Fudan is also because of this reason.

We have to put Shortwave Radio first as the oldest wall newspaper in Fudan. Its news is very well-informed, because before the Fudan Five-Day Journal had been published, it had already been revealed on this radio. Therefore, students with general curiosity welcome it very much. Before each issue is published, there must be many male and female students clustered together to look at it. Especially the young ladies who are a little prominent in the East Palace often squeeze in shyly. What they are most afraid of is that the secrets of their spring love will be revealed by the newspaper. On the male student side, this news is most welcomed, which is also an inevitable phenomenon. Recently, this oldest Shortwave Radio has been delayed in publishing for some reason, and many of its fresh news have been interviewed by the Xisheng wall newspaper that rose later. For example, the resolution of the Fudan board of directors this time. Before it was announced, the school authorities were extremely secretive, but the X issue of the Xisheng wall newspaper was published on

Page 30

That day, the news had been disclosed very accurately. As a result, there was not a single student who did not admire Xisheng. Also, since Xisheng published a rigorous analysis of the inside story of proletarian writers, it has aroused the response of other wall newspapers. This also has to be attributed to the efforts of Xisheng.

The East Palace Chronicles is A Fang's masterpiece. It is very moving to reveal it on schedule. According to A Cai, for this (East Palace Chronicles), I don't know how many storms have been caused. Today, Ms. A personally writes a letter to declare, and tomorrow, Ms. B sends a book to question. Sometimes, there are also unsigned ladies who send a blank note through the East Palace maid to joke. There are really a lot of such romantic notes in A Fang's drawer, making people envious. It's a pity that it's not a love letter, otherwise, if it were published, A Fang could get considerable remuneration because he actually spent a lot of effort writing this (East Palace Chronicles). However, A Fang also has many things to be comforted by, that is, the great reputation of (East Palace Reporter) that he bears has not only caused a sensation throughout Fudan, even the palace masters of various palaces at sea have not heard his great name and have been overwhelmed.

The Xisheng wall newspaper has made many contributions this semester. Based on the wall newspapers of the entire Fudan school, its achievements account for the top. This can also be said to be the unanimous praise of Fudan students. There are more than a dozen members of the society, but their names are kept secret. It's really a medicine in a silent gourd, and I don't know when they will be willing to announce it. However, they can have such a spirit to run a wall newspaper, and they can achieve such excellent results in a very short period of time. It is really worth envying outsiders.

The school is about to give a holiday, and the students are actively preparing for the semester exam. Therefore, the members of the Xisheng Society held a tea party at 7 pm last night (Wednesday). There were eighteen attendees. Huang Huanruo reported on the establishment and work of the society. Secondly, Diao Shenghe reported that the editing policy was eloquent and very moving. Finally, the specific plan for the next semester was discussed, and the result was very satisfactory. Li Jushi was elected as the preparation committee to plan everything during the winter vacation so that the first tea party can be held next year when school starts and continue to discuss and actively proceed. It was also decided to widely recruit members who have the same purpose as the society to strengthen the development of the society. Within a considerable range, it is planned to publish a ten-day journal dedicated to members to publish their research on literary and artistic insights. As a result, the Xisheng Society next year will definitely have a new atmosphere.

The entertainment was A Fang's report on the lustful history of the East Palace, which was very interesting and caused the members sitting to laugh. It is a pity that A Fang will wear a bachelor's hat this semester. I don't know who will take over the East Palace Chronicles next year. This makes me very worried. Although the society is full of talents, only A Fang can be qualified for the position of East Palace reporter. This is what everyone agrees on, right?

Friends, wait and see, please look forward to the new look of the Xisheng wall newspaper next year.

Reading "Manshu's Spring Dream"

— Jiang Feng

Modern West Lake is like a modern girl—although her hair is black and her eyes are as bright as paint and she has not lost her Chinese flavor, she also has high-heeled leather shoes and a short skirt. Modern West Lake is foreign houses, roads, cars, and speedboats, no longer the ancient costume of Xizi. But in the shade of Gushan, facing the smoke on a lotus pond, the trees are lush, the birds sing in unison, the clusters are messy, and wildflowers are everywhere. It is still as quiet as the Land of Peach Blossoms in troubled times and has not been affected by the times at all. It is in this place that our unparalleled talented person, Su Manshu, is buried. Manshu is living in seclusion in this place, living in seclusion in this place forever. The cuckoo on the branch, the cricket in the grass, the bright moon in the mountain, and the clear breeze on the lake are his most beloved. He did not die mediocrely like the monks called him a wonderful person. He escaped from the human world that was incompatible with him, escaped from the utilitarian and vulgar monastery, and took refuge in his own field. If you don't believe it, go ask the cuckoo on the bodhi tree that shades his soil, he will tell you the news of our poet.

One day, a red-eyed poet came to the lake. His eyes were reddened by tears, alcohol, and candy. He stumbled to the lake and listened to the news of Manshu from the cuckoo. He often lay alone in the empty mountains under a bodhi tree, with Manshu's tomb as a pillow, shedding tears, tears first reaching under the yellow earth and dissolving with Manshu's poetic bones. From then on, in addition to the clear breeze, bright moon, cricket, and cuckoo, Manshu had one more confidant. Our poet Yan Meng became Manshu's confidant. Although Manshu could not face him and chew on the camellia that the woman he loved most, this was a regrettable thing.

The two of them are from the same hometown, have the same experiences, and have the same personalities. When Manshu was having a spring dream in the tomb, Yan Meng was having a spring dream in the world. Or it can be said that Manshu's incarnation was continuing to have the spring dream in the world. The pitiful Yan Meng wrote his poetic drama (Manshu's Spring Dream) with his bitter tears, line by line, following the jump of his heart. It is warm, bitter, and overflowing with true emotions everywhere. Yan Meng is simply a stubborn beggar. He is now stretching out his poetic palm to ask for human sympathy. Mr. Liu Yazi (hopes to revive Manshu's temperament and pass it down with Mr. Yan (Meng)'s romantic poetic talent). Now Mr. Liu should be weeping with old tears and seeing his old friend Manshu resurrected in front of his eyes in the tears.

Youth Garden Guidelines

(1) The text should be about the discussion of youth issues, domestic and foreign school or student news, essays, descriptions of school life, etc., and the style is not limited.

(2) The pictures should be limited to those related to youth issues.

(3) Photos of youth life (such as sports, travel, excursions, theater, speeches, gatherings, exhibitions, various competitions, etc.), school news, and youth movements are eligible, whether individual or group.

(4) Do not write on both sides of the manuscript paper.

(5) Each article should not exceed 2,000 words.

(6) Do not write horizontally in the manuscript. Do not be sloppy in the words. Western words can be omitted if possible. If it is necessary to quote Kang Wen, it must be attached to the translation.

(7) Do not use blue ink to draw the pictures, and do not use colored paper. Use white paper and black drawing.

(8) Please indicate the Youth Garden Editorial Department on the submissions.

(9) All submissions will not be returned, whether published or not. If a return is required, it should be stated in advance.

(10) Compensation is divided into three types: three yuan, two yuan, and one yuan per thousand words of text. Pictures and photos are also the same as this example. If there are special submissions, the compensation will be calculated separately.
